	develop_780_aluminium_deposits = { #780
		
		icon = aluminium

		allowed = {
			
		}
		highlight_states = {
			highlight_state_targets = {
				state = 780
			}
		}
		available = {
			has_tech = excavation1
			num_of_civilian_factories_available_for_projects > 1
			owns_state = 780
			controls_state = 780
		}

		visible = {
			owns_state = 780
			controls_state = 780
			780 = {
				NOT = {
					has_state_flag = aluminium_780_developed_1
				}
			}
		}

		fire_only_once = yes

		cost = 10
		days_remove = 60

		modifier = {
			civilian_factory_use = 2
		}

		ai_will_do = {
			factor = 1
		}
		remove_effect = { 
			780 = { set_state_flag = aluminium_780_developed_1 } 
			780 = {
				add_resource = {
					type = aluminium
					amount = 20
				}
			}
		}	
	}
